## Thresholds Used
| Threshold | Value | What it means |
|-----------|-------|----------------|
| Min SQN | **1.0** | System Quality Number — consistency of returns. 1.0 = minimum viable; ≥2.0 = excellent. |
| Min Profit Factor | **1.5** | Gross profit ÷ gross loss. 1.5 = earn $1.50 per $1 lost. Below 1.0 = net loser. |
| Min # Trades | **10** | Minimum trades per combo — filters out statistically meaningless results. |
| Min Win Rate (%) | **30.0** | % of trades that close in profit. Low is OK if winners are much larger than losers. |
| Min Sharpe | **0.5** | Risk-adjusted return. 0.5 = acceptable; ≥1.0 = good; ≥2.0 = exceptional. |
